# Scope: country
try_steal_resources = {
    random_list = {
        # Nothing stolen...
        10 = {
            modifier = {
                factor = 1.5
                event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                    any_pop = {
                        is_intelligencer_has_purpose_disclose_spies = yes
                        is_appointed_intelligencer = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 2
                event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                    any_pop = {
                        is_intelligencer_has_purpose_disclose_spies = yes
                        is_appointed_intelligencer = yes
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_1 = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 2.5
                event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                    any_pop = {
                        is_intelligencer_has_purpose_disclose_spies = yes
                        is_appointed_intelligencer = yes
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_2 = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 3
                event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                    any_pop = {
                        is_intelligencer_has_purpose_disclose_spies = yes
                        is_appointed_intelligencer = yes
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_3 = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 3.5
                event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                    any_pop = {
                        is_intelligencer_has_purpose_disclose_spies = yes
                        is_appointed_intelligencer = yes
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_4 = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 4
                event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                    any_pop = {
                        is_intelligencer_has_purpose_disclose_spies = yes
                        is_appointed_intelligencer = yes
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_5 = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 5
                event_target:espionage_target_country = {
                    is_fallen_empire = yes
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0.1
                event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                    NOT = {
                        any_pop = {
                            is_intelligencer = yes
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_origin_country = {
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_NONE_GAINED
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_NONE_GAINED_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = ORIGIN_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_origin_planet }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_COUNTRY scope = event_target:espionage_target_country }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet }
                }
            }
            log = ">>> try_steal_resources effect: nothing was gained"
        }
        # Stolen food mult
        10 = {
            modifier = {
                factor = 1.05
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_1 = yes
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 1.1
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_2 = yes
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 1.15
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_3 = yes
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 1.2

                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 1.25
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_5 = yes
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_origin_country = {
                add_monthly_resource_mult = {
                    resource = food
                    value = @tier1materialreward
                    min = @tier1materialmin
                    max = @tier1materialmax
                }
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_GAINED_FOOD
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_GAINED_FOOD_MULT_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = ORIGIN_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_origin_planet }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_COUNTRY scope = event_target:espionage_target_country }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet }
                }
            }
            log = ">>> try_steal_resources effect: monthly food mult was gained"
        }

            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                event_target:espionage_target_country = {
                    has_country_resource = {
                        type = tiberium
                        amount < 2000
                    }
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0.5
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    is_intelligencer_not_ranked = yes
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_country = {
                add_resource = {
                    tiberium = -2000
                }
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_STOLE_TIBERIUM
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_STOLE_TIBERIUM_X2000_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_origin_country = {
                add_resource = {
                    tiberium = 2000
                }
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_GAINED_TIBERIUM
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_GAINED_TIBERIUM_X2000_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = ORIGIN_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_origin_planet }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_COUNTRY scope = event_target:espionage_target_country }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet }
                }
            }
            log = ">>> try_steal_resources effect: 2000 tiberium was stolen"

                }

                factor = 1.15

                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 1.2
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_4 = yes
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 1.25
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_5 = yes
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_origin_country = {
                add_monthly_resource_mult = {
                    resource = elerium
                    value = @tier1materialreward
                    min = @tier1materialmin
                    max = @tier1materialmax
                }
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_GAINED_ELERIUM
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_GAINED_ELERIUM_MULT_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = ORIGIN_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_origin_planet }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_COUNTRY scope = event_target:espionage_target_country }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet }
                }
            }
            log = ">>> try_steal_resources effect: monthly elerium mult was gained"

                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet }
                }
            }
            log = ">>> try_steal_resources effect: 10000 kryptonite was stolen"
        }
        # Slolen 20000 kryptonite
        5 = {
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                event_target:espionage_target_country = {
                    has_country_resource = {
                        type = kryptonite
                        amount < 20000
                    }
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    NOR = {
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_4 = yes
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_5 = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_country = {
                add_resource = {
                    kryptonite = -20000
                }
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_STOLE_KRYPTONITE
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_STOLE_KRYPTONITE_X20000_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_origin_country = {
                add_resource = {
                    kryptonite = 20000
                }
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_GAINED_KRYPTONITE
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_GAINED_KRYPTONITE_X20000_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = ORIGIN_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_origin_planet }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_COUNTRY scope = event_target:espionage_target_country }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet }
                }
            }
            log = ">>> try_steal_resources effect: 20000 kryptonite was stolen"
        }
        # Slolen 40000 kryptonite
        5 = {
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                event_target:espionage_target_country = {
                    has_country_resource = {
                        type = kryptonite
                        amount < 40000
                    }
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    NOT = {
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_5 = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_country = {
